Waves and the ocean not only provide a source of movement and randomness, but also align with Portugalâs maritime history and the officeâs scenic view.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;However, this was easier said than done. It turns out that making a wave machine wall is a real challenge, given that these toys are not as popular as they were in the past,Â  and arenât being manufactured in the size we needed any more. We scoured eBay and other sources but couldn&amp;#39;t find enough, consistent in style and in working order wave machines. We also discovered that off-the-shelf models werenât designed to run 24/7, which was a critical requirement for our use.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4&gt;Artistry to create wave machines&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;Undaunted, &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/cloudflare-top-100-most-loved-workplaces-in-2022\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Cloudflareâs Places team&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, which ensures our offices reflect our values and culture, found a &lt;a href=\&quot;https://wavemotionmachines.com/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;U.S.-based artisan&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; that specializes in ocean wave displays to create the wave machines for us. Since 2009, his one-person business, &lt;a href=\&quot;https://wavemotionmachines.com/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Hughes Wave Motion Machines&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, has blended artistry, engineering, and research, following his transition from Lockheed Martin Space Systems, where he designed military and commercial satellites.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div style=\&quot;position: relative; padding-top: 56.25%;\&quot;&gt;\n  &lt;iframe\n    src=\&quot;https://customer-eq7kiuol0tk9chox.cloudflarestream.com/82638d9e81c68911d07fc2a0db093b74/iframe?muted=true&amp;preload=true&amp;poster=https%3A%2F%2Fcustomer-eq7kiuol0tk9chox.cloudflarestream.com%2F82638d9e81c68911d07fc2a0db093b74%2Fthumbnails%2Fthumbnail.jpg%3Ftime%3D%26height%3D600\&quot;\n    loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;\n    style=\&quot;border: none; position: absolute; top: 0; left: 0; height: 100%; width: 100%;\&quot;\n    allow=\&quot;accelerometer; gyroscope; autoplay; encrypted-media; picture-in-picture;\&quot;\n    allowfullscreen=\&quot;true\&quot;\n  &gt;&lt;/iframe&gt;\n&lt;/div&gt;\n&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;sup&gt;&lt;i&gt;Timelapse of the mesmerizing office waves, set to the tune of an AI-generated song.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Collaborating closely, we developed a custom rectangular wave machine (18 inches/45 cm long) that runs nonstop â not an easy task â which required hundreds of hours of testing and many iterations. Featuring rotating wheels, continuous motors, and a unique fluid formula, these machines create realistic ocean-like waves in green, blue, and Cloudflareâs signature orange.Â &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Hereâs a quote from the artist himself about these wave machines:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;blockquote&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;âThe machineâs design is a balancing act of matching components and their placement to how the fluid responds in a given configuration. There is a complex yet delicate relationship between viscosity, specific gravity, the size and design of the vessel, and the placement of each mechanical interface. Everything must be precisely aligned, centered around the fluid like a mathematical function. I like to say itâs akin to âbalancing a checkerboard on a beach ball in the wind.ââ&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/blockquote&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/3K9fpTU0D0xi831MHFOFBj/570b8c307fea1078f3c0262e13447bf6/image7.jpg\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1500\&quot; height=\&quot;1999\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;sup&gt;&lt;i&gt;The Cloudflare Places Team with Lisbon office architects and contractor testing wave machine placement, shelves, lighting, and mirrors to enhance movement and reflection, March 2024.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Despite delays, the Lisbon wave machines finally debuted on March 10, 2025 â an incredibly exciting moment for the Places team.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Some numbers about our wave-machine entropy wall:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;50 wave machines, 50 motion wheels &amp;amp; motors, 50 acrylic containers filled with Hughes Wave Fluid Formula (two &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.sciencedirect.com/topics/engineering/immiscible-liquid\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;immiscible liquids&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;3 liquid colors: blue, green, and orange&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;15 months from concept to completion&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;14 flips (side-to-side balancing movements) per minute â over 20,000 per day&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;Over 15 waves per minute&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;~0.5 liters of liquid per machine&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;\n          &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n            &lt;h3 id=\&quot;lavarand-origins-and-walls-of-entropy\&quot;&gt;LavaRand origins and walls of entropy&lt;/h3&gt;\n            &lt;a href=\&quot;#lavarand-origins-and-walls-of-entropy\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-left-5\&quot;&gt;\n              &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n            &lt;/a&gt;\n          &lt;/div&gt;\n        &lt;p&gt;Cloudflareâs servers handle 71 million HTTP requests per second on average, with 100 million HTTP requests per second at peak. &lt;a href=\&quot;https://radar.cloudflare.com/adoption-and-usage#http-vs-https\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Most of these requests are secured via TLS&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, which relies on secure randomness for cryptographic integrity. A Cryptographically Secure Pseudorandom Number Generator (&lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.cloudflare.com/learning/ssl/lava-lamp-encryption/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;CSPRNG&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;) ensures unpredictability, but only when seeded with high-quality entropy. Since chaotic movement in the real world is truly random, Cloudflare designed a system to harness it. Our &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/harnessing-office-chaos/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;2024 blog post&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; expands on this topic in a more technical way, but hereâs a quick summary.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;In &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/randomness-101-lavarand-in-production/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;2017&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, Cloudflare launched LavaRand, inspired by &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.wired.com/1997/03/lava-lites-easy-to-break-hard-to-crack/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Silicon Graphicsâ 1997 concept&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; However, the need for randomness in security was already a hot topic on our blog before that, such as in our discussions of &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/why-randomness-matters/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;securing systems&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; and &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/a-relatively-easy-to-understand-primer-on-elliptic-curve-cryptography/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;cryptography&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. Originally, LavaRand collected entropy from a wall of lava lamps in our San Francisco office, feeding an internal API that servers periodically query to include in their entropy pools. Over time, we expanded LavaRand beyond lava lamps, incorporating &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/harnessing-office-chaos/#londons-unpredictable-pendulums\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;new sources of office chaos&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; while maintaining the same core method.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/2v6Wvde8j8R7482QjBsSrV/89b37c652654e27c13d328e9acac6489/image9.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1612\&quot; height=\&quot;381\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;A camera captures images of dynamic, unpredictable randomness displays. Shadows, lighting changes, and even sensor noise contribute entropy. Each image is then processed into a compact hash, converting it into a sequence of random bytes. These, combined with the previous seed and local system entropy, serve as input for a Key Derivation Function (&lt;a href=\&quot;https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Key_derivation_function\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;KDF&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;), which generates a new seed for a CSPRNG â capable of producing virtually unlimited random bytes upon request. The waves in our Lisbon office are now contributing to this pool of randomness.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/1XFFjr4jhRMQlz6akHKZm4/44759c4e879de3792cd21b4ce2525c90/image5.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1491\&quot; height=\&quot;400\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;Cloudflareâs LavaRand API makes this randomness accessible internally, strengthening cryptographic security across our global infrastructure. For example, when you use &lt;i&gt;Math.random()&lt;/i&gt; in &lt;a href=\&quot;https://workers.cloudflare.com/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Cloudflare Workers&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, part of that randomness comes from LavaRand. Similarly, querying our &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/harnessing-office-chaos/#drand-distributed-and-verifiable-public-randomness\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;drand API&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; taps into LavaRand as well. Cloudflare offers this API to enable anyone to generate random numbers and even seed their own systems.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n            &lt;h3 id=\&quot;our-new-lisbon-office-space\&quot;&gt;Our new Lisbon office space&lt;/h3&gt;\n            &lt;a href=\&quot;#our-new-lisbon-office-space\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-left-5\&quot;&gt;\n              &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n            &lt;/a&gt;\n          &lt;/div&gt;\n        \n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/5ivPkCfTkGxfo6Swt6p9qY/e7414a14b88bef7ac7e0ef6f737b58c6/image8.jpg\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1999\&quot; height=\&quot;1330\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;sup&gt;&lt;i&gt;Photo of the view from our Lisbon office, featuring ceiling lights arranged in a wave-like pattern.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Entropy also inspired the design ethos of our new Lisbon office, given that the wall of waves and the office are part of the same project. As soon as you enter, you&amp;#39;re greeted not only by the motion of the entropy wall but also by the constant movement of planet Earth on our Cloudflare Radar Display screen that stands next to it. But the waves donât stop there â more elements throughout the space mimic the dynamic flow of the Internet itself. Unlike ocean tides, however, Internet traffic ebbs and flows with the motion of the Sun, not the Moon.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;As you walk through the office, waves are everywhere â in the ceiling lights, the architectural contours, and even the floor plan, thoughtfully designed by our architect to reflect the fluid movement of water. The visual elements create a cohesive experience, reinforcing a sense of motion. Each meeting room embraces this maritime theme, named after famous Portuguese beaches â including, naturally, NazarÃ©.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;We partnered with an incredible group of local Portuguese vendors for this construction project, where all the leads were women â something incredibly rare for the industry. The local teams worked with passion, proudly wore Cloudflare t-shirts, and fostered a warm, family-like atmosphere. They openly expressed pride in the project, sharing how it stood out from anything they had worked on before.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/7lpuurEtWfpIPKvHVqmD0L/0b0561097859f286d6b5e98db82f1e0f/image3.jpg\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1999\&quot; height=\&quot;1125\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;sup&gt;&lt;i&gt;Our amazing third-party team and internal Places team, proudly rocking Cloudflare shirts after bringing this project to life.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n            &lt;h3 id=\&quot;help-us-select-a-name-for-our-new-wall-of-entropy\&quot;&gt;Help us select a name for our new wall of entropy&lt;/h3&gt;\n            &lt;a href=\&quot;#help-us-select-a-name-for-our-new-wall-of-entropy\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-left-5\&quot;&gt;\n              &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n            &lt;/a&gt;\n          &lt;/div&gt;\n        &lt;p&gt;Next, we have several name options for this new wall of entropy. recently, this new wall of entropy began with an idea back in 2023: âWhat could we use for randomness that was like our lava lamp wall in San Francisco but represented our team in Portugal?â&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The original inspiration came from wave motion machine desk toys, which were popular among some of our team members. Waves and the ocean not only provide a source of movement and randomness, but also align with Portugalâs maritime history and the officeâs scenic view.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;However, this was easier said than done. It turns out that making a wave machine wall is a real challenge, given that these toys are not as popular as they were in the past,Â  and arenât being manufactured in the size we needed any more. We scoured eBay and other sources but couldn&amp;#39;t find enough, consistent in style and in working order wave machines. We also discovered that off-the-shelf models werenât designed to run 24/7, which was a critical requirement for our use.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4&gt;Artistry to create wave machines&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;Undaunted, &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/cloudflare-top-100-most-loved-workplaces-in-2022\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Cloudflareâs Places team&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, which ensures our offices reflect our values and culture, found a &lt;a href=\&quot;https://wavemotionmachines.com/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;U.S.-based artisan&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; that specializes in ocean wave displays to create the wave machines for us. Since 2009, his one-person business, &lt;a href=\&quot;https://wavemotionmachines.com/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Hughes Wave Motion Machines&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, has blended artistry, engineering, and research, following his transition from Lockheed Martin Space Systems, where he designed military and commercial satellites.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div style=\&quot;position: relative; padding-top: 56.25%;\&quot;&gt;\n  &lt;iframe\n    src=\&quot;https://customer-eq7kiuol0tk9chox.cloudflarestream.com/82638d9e81c68911d07fc2a0db093b74/iframe?muted=true&amp;preload=true&amp;poster=https%3A%2F%2Fcustomer-eq7kiuol0tk9chox.cloudflarestream.com%2F82638d9e81c68911d07fc2a0db093b74%2Fthumbnails%2Fthumbnail.jpg%3Ftime%3D%26height%3D600\&quot;\n    loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;\n    style=\&quot;border: none; position: absolute; top: 0; left: 0; height: 100%; width: 100%;\&quot;\n    allow=\&quot;accelerometer; gyroscope; autoplay; encrypted-media; picture-in-picture;\&quot;\n    allowfullscreen=\&quot;true\&quot;\n  &gt;&lt;/iframe&gt;\n&lt;/div&gt;\n&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;sup&gt;&lt;i&gt;Timelapse of the mesmerizing office waves, set to the tune of an AI-generated song.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Collaborating closely, we developed a custom rectangular wave machine (18 inches/45 cm long) that runs nonstop â not an easy task â which required hundreds of hours of testing and many iterations. Featuring rotating wheels, continuous motors, and a unique fluid formula, these machines create realistic ocean-like waves in green, blue, and Cloudflareâs signature orange.Â &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Hereâs a quote from the artist himself about these wave machines:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;blockquote&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;âThe machineâs design is a balancing act of matching components and their placement to how the fluid responds in a given configuration. There is a complex yet delicate relationship between viscosity, specific gravity, the size and design of the vessel, and the placement of each mechanical interface. Everything must be precisely aligned, centered around the fluid like a mathematical function. I like to say itâs akin to âbalancing a checkerboard on a beach ball in the wind.ââ&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/blockquote&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/3K9fpTU0D0xi831MHFOFBj/570b8c307fea1078f3c0262e13447bf6/image7.jpg\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1500\&quot; height=\&quot;1999\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;sup&gt;&lt;i&gt;The Cloudflare Places Team with Lisbon office architects and contractor testing wave machine placement, shelves, lighting, and mirrors to enhance movement and reflection, March 2024.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Despite delays, the Lisbon wave machines finally debuted on March 10, 2025 â an incredibly exciting moment for the Places team.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Some numbers about our wave-machine entropy wall:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;50 wave machines, 50 motion wheels &amp;amp; motors, 50 acrylic containers filled with Hughes Wave Fluid Formula (two &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.sciencedirect.com/topics/engineering/immiscible-liquid\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;immiscible liquids&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;3 liquid colors: blue, green, and orange&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;15 months from concept to completion&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;14 flips (side-to-side balancing movements) per minute â over 20,000 per day&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;Over 15 waves per minute&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;~0.5 liters of liquid per machine&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;\n          &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n            &lt;h3 id=\&quot;lavarand-origins-and-walls-of-entropy\&quot;&gt;LavaRand origins and walls of entropy&lt;/h3&gt;\n            &lt;a href=\&quot;#lavarand-origins-and-walls-of-entropy\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-left-5\&quot;&gt;\n              &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n            &lt;/a&gt;\n          &lt;/div&gt;\n        &lt;p&gt;Cloudflareâs servers handle 71 million HTTP requests per second on average, with 100 million HTTP requests per second at peak. &lt;a href=\&quot;https://radar.cloudflare.com/adoption-and-usage#http-vs-https\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Most of these requests are secured via TLS&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, which relies on secure randomness for cryptographic integrity. A Cryptographically Secure Pseudorandom Number Generator (&lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.cloudflare.com/learning/ssl/lava-lamp-encryption/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;CSPRNG&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;) ensures unpredictability, but only when seeded with high-quality entropy. Since chaotic movement in the real world is truly random, Cloudflare designed a system to harness it. Our &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/harnessing-office-chaos/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;2024 blog post&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; expands on this topic in a more technical way, but hereâs a quick summary.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;In &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/randomness-101-lavarand-in-production/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;2017&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, Cloudflare launched LavaRand, inspired by &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.wired.com/1997/03/lava-lites-easy-to-break-hard-to-crack/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Silicon Graphicsâ 1997 concept&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; However, the need for randomness in security was already a hot topic on our blog before that, such as in our discussions of &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/why-randomness-matters/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;securing systems&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; and &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/a-relatively-easy-to-understand-primer-on-elliptic-curve-cryptography/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;cryptography&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. Originally, LavaRand collected entropy from a wall of lava lamps in our San Francisco office, feeding an internal API that servers periodically query to include in their entropy pools. Over time, we expanded LavaRand beyond lava lamps, incorporating &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/harnessing-office-chaos/#londons-unpredictable-pendulums\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;new sources of office chaos&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; while maintaining the same core method.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/2v6Wvde8j8R7482QjBsSrV/89b37c652654e27c13d328e9acac6489/image9.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1612\&quot; height=\&quot;381\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;A camera captures images of dynamic, unpredictable randomness displays. Shadows, lighting changes, and even sensor noise contribute entropy. Each image is then processed into a compact hash, converting it into a sequence of random bytes. These, combined with the previous seed and local system entropy, serve as input for a Key Derivation Function (&lt;a href=\&quot;https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Key_derivation_function\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;KDF&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;), which generates a new seed for a CSPRNG â capable of producing virtually unlimited random bytes upon request. The waves in our Lisbon office are now contributing to this pool of randomness.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/1XFFjr4jhRMQlz6akHKZm4/44759c4e879de3792cd21b4ce2525c90/image5.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1491\&quot; height=\&quot;400\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;Cloudflareâs LavaRand API makes this randomness accessible internally, strengthening cryptographic security across our global infrastructure. For example, when you use &lt;i&gt;Math.random()&lt;/i&gt; in &lt;a href=\&quot;https://workers.cloudflare.com/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Cloudflare Workers&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, part of that randomness comes from LavaRand. Similarly, querying our &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/harnessing-office-chaos/#drand-distributed-and-verifiable-public-randomness\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;drand API&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; taps into LavaRand as well. Cloudflare offers this API to enable anyone to generate random numbers and even seed their own systems.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n            &lt;h3 id=\&quot;our-new-lisbon-office-space\&quot;&gt;Our new Lisbon office space&lt;/h3&gt;\n            &lt;a href=\&quot;#our-new-lisbon-office-space\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-left-5\&quot;&gt;\n              &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n            &lt;/a&gt;\n          &lt;/div&gt;\n        \n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/5ivPkCfTkGxfo6Swt6p9qY/e7414a14b88bef7ac7e0ef6f737b58c6/image8.jpg\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1999\&quot; height=\&quot;1330\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;sup&gt;&lt;i&gt;Photo of the view from our Lisbon office, featuring ceiling lights arranged in a wave-like pattern.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Entropy also inspired the design ethos of our new Lisbon office, given that the wall of waves and the office are part of the same project. As soon as you enter, you&amp;#39;re greeted not only by the motion of the entropy wall but also by the constant movement of planet Earth on our Cloudflare Radar Display screen that stands next to it. But the waves donât stop there â more elements throughout the space mimic the dynamic flow of the Internet itself. Unlike ocean tides, however, Internet traffic ebbs and flows with the motion of the Sun, not the Moon.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;As you walk through the office, waves are everywhere â in the ceiling lights, the architectural contours, and even the floor plan, thoughtfully designed by our architect to reflect the fluid movement of water. The visual elements create a cohesive experience, reinforcing a sense of motion. Each meeting room embraces this maritime theme, named after famous Portuguese beaches â including, naturally, NazarÃ©.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;We partnered with an incredible group of local Portuguese vendors for this construction project, where all the leads were women â something incredibly rare for the industry. The local teams worked with passion, proudly wore Cloudflare t-shirts, and fostered a warm, family-like atmosphere. They openly expressed pride in the project, sharing how it stood out from anything they had worked on before.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/7lpuurEtWfpIPKvHVqmD0L/0b0561097859f286d6b5e98db82f1e0f/image3.jpg\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1999\&quot; height=\&quot;1125\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;sup&gt;&lt;i&gt;Our amazing third-party team and internal Places team, proudly rocking Cloudflare shirts after bringing this project to life.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n            &lt;h3 id=\&quot;help-us-select-a-name-for-our-new-wall-of-entropy\&quot;&gt;Help us select a name for our new wall of entropy&lt;/h3&gt;\n            &lt;a href=\&quot;#help-us-select-a-name-for-our-new-wall-of-entropy\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-left-5\&quot;&gt;\n              &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n            &lt;/a&gt;\n          &lt;/div&gt;\n        &lt;p&gt;Next, we have several name options for this new wall of entropy. updates&quot;],&quot;slug&quot;:[0,&quot;enhanced-security-and-simplified-controls-with-automated-botnet-protection&quot;],&quot;excerpt&quot;:[0,&quot;Enhanced security, simplified control! This Security Week, Cloudflare unveils automated botnet protection, flexible cipher suites, and an upgraded URL Scanner.&quot;],&quot;featured&quot;:[0,false],&quot;html&quot;:[0,&quot;&lt;p&gt;At Cloudflare, we are constantly innovating and launching new features and capabilities across our product portfolio. Today, we&amp;#39;re releasing a number of new features aimed at improving the security tools available to our customers.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Automated security level: &lt;/b&gt;Cloudflareâs Security Level setting has been improved and no longer requires manual configuration. By integrating botnet data along with other request rate signals, all customers are protected from confirmed known malicious botnet traffic without any action required.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Cipher suite selection:&lt;/b&gt; You now have greater control over encryption settings via the Cloudflare dashboard, including specific cipher suite selection based on our client or compliance requirements.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Improved URL scanner:&lt;/b&gt; New features include bulk scanning, similarity search, location picker and more.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;These updates are designed to give you more power and flexibility when managing online security, from proactive threat detection to granular control over encryption settings.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n            &lt;h3 id=\&quot;automating-security-level-to-provide-stronger-protection-for-all\&quot;&gt;Automating Security Level to provide stronger protection for all&lt;/h3&gt;\n            &lt;a href=\&quot;#automating-security-level-to-provide-stronger-protection-for-all\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-left-5\&quot;&gt;\n              &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n            &lt;/a&gt;\n          &lt;/div&gt;\n        &lt;p&gt;Cloudflareâs &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/waf/tools/security-level/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Security Level feature&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; was designed to protect customer websites from malicious activity.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Available to all Cloudflare customers, including the free tier, it has always had very simple logic: if a connecting client IP address has shown malicious behavior across our network, issue a &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/waf/reference/cloudflare-challenges/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;managed challenge&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. The system tracks malicious behavior by assigning a threat score to each IP address. The more bad behavior is observed, the higher the score. Cloudflare customers could configure &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/waf/tools/security-level/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;the threshold that would trigger the challenge&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;We are now announcing an update to how Security Level works, by combining the IP address threat signal with threshold and botnet data. The resulting detection improvements have allowed us to automate the configuration, no longer requiring customers to set a threshold.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/1RFWQl2Da9xu9MdfbJCRhy/8750770351d124ecf8d2f2b274f2e3cc/image1.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1392\&quot; height=\&quot;472\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;The Security Level setting is now &lt;b&gt;Always protected&lt;/b&gt; in the dashboard, and ip_threat_score fields in WAF Custom Rules will no longer be populated. No change is required by Cloudflare customers. The &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/fundamentals/reference/under-attack-mode/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;âI am under attackâ&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; option remains unchanged.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n            &lt;h3 id=\&quot;stronger-protection-by-default-for-all-customers\&quot;&gt;Stronger protection, by default, for all customers&lt;/h3&gt;\n            &lt;a href=\&quot;#stronger-protection-by-default-for-all-customers\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-left-5\&quot;&gt;\n              &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n            &lt;/a&gt;\n          &lt;/div&gt;\n        &lt;p&gt;Although we always favor simplicity, privacy-related services, including our own WARP, have seen growing use. Meanwhile, &lt;a href=\&quot;https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Carrier-grade_NAT\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;carrier-grade network address translation (CGNATs)&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; and outbound forward proxies have been widely used for many years.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;These services often result in multiple users sharing the same IP address, which can lead to legitimate users being challenged unfairly since individual addresses donât strictly correlate with unique client behavior. Moreover, threat actors have become increasingly adept at anonymizing and dynamically changing their IP addresses using tools like VPNs, proxies, and botnets, further diminishing the reliability of IP addresses as a standalone indicator of malicious activity. Recognising these limitations, it was time for us to revisit Security Levelâs logic to reduce the number of false positives being observed.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;In February 2024, we introduced a new security system that automatically combines the real-time DDoS score with a traffic threshold and a botnet tracking system. The real-time DDoS score is part of our autonomous DDoS detection system, which analyzes traffic patterns to identify potential threats. This system superseded and replaced the existing Security Level logic, and is deployed on all customer traffic, including free plans. After thorough monitoring and analysis over the past year, we have confirmed that these behavior-based mitigation systems provide more accurate results. Notably, we&amp;#39;ve observed a significant reduction in false positives, demonstrating the limitations of the previous IP address-only logic.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4&gt;Better botnet tracking&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;Our new logic combines IP address signals with behavioral and threshold indicators to improve the accuracy of botnet detection. While IP addresses alone can be unreliable due to potential false positives, we enhance their utility by integrating them with additional signals. We monitor surges in traffic from known &amp;quot;bad&amp;quot; IP addresses and further refine this data by examining specific properties such as path, accept, and host headers.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;We also introduced a new botnet tracking system that continuously detects and tracks botnet activity across the Cloudflare network. From our unique vantage point as a &lt;a href=\&quot;https://w3techs.com/technologies/overview/proxy\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;reverse proxy for nearly 20% of all websites&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, we maintain a dynamic database of IP addresses associated with botnet activity. This database is continuously updated, enabling us to automatically respond to emerging threats without manual intervention. This effect is visible in the &lt;a href=\&quot;https://radar.cloudflare.com/security-and-attacks?dateStart=2024-02-01&amp;dateEnd=2024-03-31#mitigated-traffic-sources\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Cloudflare Radar chart&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; below, as we saw sharp growth in DDoS mitigations in February 2024 as the botnet tracking system was implemented.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/3yOP8zoC5ZLVi4WHnXI0jH/ef3fd6ad10e8357b6b4f1bfb90e6d6b6/image4.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;Growth in DDoS mitigations starting February 2024 as the botnet tracking system was released\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1600\&quot; height=\&quot;900\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;h4&gt;What it means for our customers and their users&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;Customers now get better protection while having to manage fewer configurations, and they can rest assured that their online presence remains fully protected. These security measures are integrated and enabled by default across all of our plans, ensuring protection without the need for manual configuration or rule management.\nThis improvement is particularly beneficial for users accessing sites through proxy services or CGNATs, as these setups can sometimes trigger unnecessary security checks, potentially disrupting access to websites.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4&gt;Whatâs next&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;Our team is looking at defining the next generation of threat scoring mechanisms. This initiative aims to provide our customers with more relevant and effective controls and tools to combat today&amp;#39;s and tomorrow&amp;#39;s potential security threats.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Effective March 17, 2025, we are removing the option to configure manual rules using the threat score parameter in the Cloudflare dashboard. The &amp;quot;I&amp;#39;m Under Attack&amp;quot; mode remains available, allowing users to issue managed challenges to all traffic when needed.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;By the end of Q1 2026, we anticipate disabling all rules that rely on IP threat score. This means that using the threat score parameter in the Rulesets API and via Terraform wonât be available after the end of the transition period. However, we encourage customers to be proactive and edit or remove the rules containing the threat score parameter starting today.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n            &lt;h3 id=\&quot;cipher-suite-selection-now-available-in-the-ui\&quot;&gt;Cipher suite selection now available in the UI&lt;/h3&gt;\n            &lt;a href=\&quot;#cipher-suite-selection-now-available-in-the-ui\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-left-5\&quot;&gt;\n              &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n            &lt;/a&gt;\n          &lt;/div&gt;\n        \n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/2e5Q0ghzpkuTQrR335fzIa/156b9531735fd9164768970fd08f5f85/image5.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1999\&quot; height=\&quot;497\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;Building upon our core security features, we&amp;#39;re also giving you more control over your encryption: cipher suite selection is now available in the Cloudflare dashboard!Â &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;When a client initiates a visit to a Cloudflare-protected website, a &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.cloudflare.com/learning/ssl/what-happens-in-a-tls-handshake/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;TLS handshake&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; occurs, where clients present a list of supported &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/ssl/edge-certificates/additional-options/cipher-suites/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;cipher suites&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; â cryptographic algorithms crucial for secure connections. While newer algorithms enhance security, balancing this with broad compatibility is key, as some customers prioritise reach by supporting older devices, even with less secure ciphers. To accommodate varied client needs, Cloudflare&amp;#39;s default settings emphasise wide compatibility, allowing customers to tailor cipher suite selection based on their priorities: strong security, compliance (PCI DSS, FIPS 140-2), or legacy device support.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Previously, customizing cipher suites required multiple API calls, proving cumbersome for many users. Now, Cloudflare introduces Cipher Suite Selection to the dashboard. This feature introduces user-friendly selection flows like security recommendations, compliance presets, and custom selections.Â Â &lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4&gt;Understanding cipher suites&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;Cipher suites are collections of cryptographic algorithms used for key exchange, authentication, encryption, and message integrity, essential for a TLS handshake. During the handshakeâs initiation, the client sends a &amp;quot;client hello&amp;quot; message containing a list of supported cipher suites. The server responds with a &amp;quot;server hello&amp;quot; message, choosing a cipher suite from the client&amp;#39;s list based on security and compatibility. This chosen cipher suite forms the basis of TLS termination and plays a crucial role in establishing a secure HTTPS connection. Hereâs a quick overview of each component:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Key exchange algorithm:&lt;/b&gt; Secures the exchange of encryption keys between parties.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Authentication algorithm:&lt;/b&gt; Verifies the identities of the communicating parties.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Encryption algorithm:&lt;/b&gt; Ensures the confidentiality of the data.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Message integrity algorithm:&lt;/b&gt; Confirms that the data remains unaltered during transmission.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/perfect-forward-secrecy/\&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Perfect forward secrecy&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;b&gt; &lt;/b&gt;is an important feature of modern cipher suites. It ensures that each session&amp;#39;s encryption keys are generated independently, which means that even if a serverâs private key is compromised in the future, past communications remain secure.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4&gt;What we are offeringÂ &lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;You can find cipher suite configuration under Edge Certificates in your zoneâs SSL/TLS dashboard. There, you will be able to view your allow-listed set of cipher suites. &lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/6fT7BvPow3zvKTl1JYw7yX/8dcd8b797f671b05211defaaf4c4bb83/image5.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1999\&quot; height=\&quot;399\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;Additionally, you will be able to choose from three different user flows, depending on your specific use case, to seamlessly select your appropriate list. Those three user flows are: security recommendation selection, compliance selection, or custom selection. The goal of the user flows is to outfit customers with cipher suites that match their goals and priorities, whether those are maximum compatibility or best possible security.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;1. Security recommendationsÂ &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;To streamline the process, we have turned our &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/ssl/reference/cipher-suites/recommendations/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;cipher suites recommendations&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; into selectable options. This is in an effort to expose our customers to cipher suites in a tangible way and enable them to choose between different security configurations and compatibility. Here is what they mean:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Modern:&lt;/b&gt; Provides the highest level of security and performance with support for Perfect Forward Secrecy and &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.ietf.org/archive/id/draft-irtf-cfrg-aead-properties-03.html\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Authenticated Encryption (AEAD)&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. Ideal for customers who prioritize top-notch security and performance, such as financial institutions, healthcare providers, or government agencies. This selection requires TLS 1.3 to be enabled and the minimum TLS version set to 1.2.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Compatible:&lt;/b&gt; Balances security and compatibility by offering forward-secret cipher suites that are broadly compatible with older systems. Suitable for most customers who need a good balance between security and reach. This selection also requires TLS 1.3 to be enabled and the minimum TLS version set to 1.2.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Legacy:&lt;/b&gt; Optimizes for the widest reach, supporting a wide range of legacy devices and systems. Best for customers who do not handle sensitive data and need to accommodate a variety of visitors. This option is ideal for blogs or organizations that rely on older systems.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;2. Compliance selection&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Additionally, we have also turned our &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/ssl/reference/cipher-suites/compliance-status/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;compliance recommendations&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; into selectable options to make it easier for our customers to meet their PCI DSS or FIPS-140-2 requirements.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.pcisecuritystandards.org/standards/pci-dss/\&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;PCI DSS Compliance:&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt; Ensures that your cipher suite selection aligns with PCI DSS standards for protecting cardholder data. This option will enforce a requirement to set a minimum TLS version of 1.2, and TLS 1.3 to be enabled, to maintain compliance.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;Since the list of supported cipher suites require TLS 1.3 to be enabled and a minimum TLS version of 1.2 in order to be compliant, we will disable compliance selection until the zone settings are updated to meet those requirements. This effort is to ensure that our customers are truly compliant and have the proper zone settings to be so.Â &lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=\&quot;https://csrc.nist.gov/pubs/fips/140-2/upd2/final\&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;FIPS 140-2 Compliance&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;u&gt;:&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; Tailored for customers needing to meet federal security standards for cryptographic modules. Ensures that your encryption practices comply with FIPS 140-2 requirements.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;3. Custom selectionÂ &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;For customers needing precise control, the custom selection flow allows individual cipher suite selection, excluding TLS 1.3 suites which are automatically enabled with TLS 1.3. To prevent disruptions, guardrails ensure compatibility by validating that the minimum TLS version aligns with the selected cipher suites and that the SSL/TLS certificate is compatible (e.g., RSA certificates require RSA cipher suites).&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n            &lt;h3 id=\&quot;api\&quot;&gt;APIÂ &lt;/h3&gt;\n            &lt;a href=\&quot;#api\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-left-5\&quot;&gt;\n              &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n            &lt;/a&gt;\n          &lt;/div&gt;\n        &lt;p&gt;The &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/ssl/edge-certificates/additional-options/cipher-suites/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;API&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; will still be available to our customers. This aims to support an existing framework, especially to customers who are already API reliant. Additionally, Cloudflare preserves the specified cipher suites in the order they are set via the API and that control of ordering will remain unique to our API offering.Â &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;With your Advanced Certificate Manager or Cloudflare for SaaS subscription, head to Edge Certificates in your zoneâs SSL dashboard and give it a try today!&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n            &lt;h3 id=\&quot;smarter-scanning-safer-internet-with-the-new-version-of-url-scanner\&quot;&gt;Smarter scanning, safer Internet with the new version of URL Scanner&lt;/h3&gt;\n            &lt;a href=\&quot;#smarter-scanning-safer-internet-with-the-new-version-of-url-scanner\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-left-5\&quot;&gt;\n              &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n            &lt;/a&gt;\n          &lt;/div&gt;\n        \n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/5eFwJMzk3JuwYNKcSk4kiH/63e4a8713be583d83df737cf6f59281d/image10.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1999\&quot; height=\&quot;450\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;Cloudflare&amp;#39;s URL Scanner is a tool designed to detect and analyze potential security threats like phishing and malware by scanning and evaluating websites, providing detailed insights into their safety and technology usage. We&amp;#39;ve leveraged our own &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/radar/investigate/url-scanner/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;URL Scanner&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; to enhance our internal &lt;u&gt;Trust &amp;amp; Safety efforts&lt;/u&gt;, automating the detection and mitigation of some forms of abuse on our platform. This has not only strengthened our own security posture, but has also directly influenced the development of the new features we&amp;#39;re announcing today.Â &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Phishing attacks are on the rise across the Internet, and we saw a major opportunity to be &amp;quot;customer zero&amp;quot; for our URL Scanner to address abuse on our own network. By working closely with our Trust &amp;amp; Safety team to understand how the URL Scanner could better identify potential phishing attempts, we&amp;#39;ve improved the speed and accuracy of our response to abuse reports, making the Internet safer for everyone. Today, we&amp;#39;re excited to share the new API version and the latest updates to URL Scanner, which include the ability to scan from specific geographic locations, bulk scanning, search by Indicators of Compromise (IOCs), improved UI and information display, comprehensive IOC listings, advanced sorting options, and more. These features are the result of our own experiences in leveraging URL Scanner to safeguard our platform and our customers, and we&amp;#39;re confident that they will prove useful to our security analysts and threat intelligence users.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4&gt;Scan up to 100 URLs at once by using bulk submissions&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;Cloudflare Enterprise customers can now conduct routine scans of their web assets to identify emerging vulnerabilities, ensuring that potential threats are addressed proactively, by using the &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/api/resources/url_scanner/subresources/scans/methods/bulk_create/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Bulk Scanning API endpoint&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. Another use case for the bulk scanning functionality is developers leveraging bulk scanning to verify that all URLs your team is accessing are secure and free from potential exploits before launching new websites or updates.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Scanning of multiple URLs addresses the specific needs of our users engaged in threat hunting. Many of them maintain extensive lists of URLs that require swift investigation to identify potential threats. Currently, they face the task of submitting these URLs one by one, which not only slows down their workflow but also increases the manual effort involved in their security processes. With the introduction of bulk submission capabilities, users can now submit up to 100 URLs at a time for scanning.Â &lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4&gt;How we built the bulk scanning feature&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;Letâs look at a regular workflow:&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/6l8aN6xhN4HEfw4ZMi1MT8/5eb62472b42f75487c55b17b3415b584/image6.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1999\&quot; height=\&quot;475\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;In this workflow, when the user submits a new scan, we create a &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/durable-objects/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Durable Object&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; with the same ID as the scan, save the scan options, like the URL to scan, to the &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/durable-objects/api/storage-api/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Durable Objectsâs storage&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; and schedule an &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/durable-objects/api/storage-api/#setalarm\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;alarm&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; for a few seconds later. This allows us to respond immediately to the user, signalling a successful submission. A few seconds later the alarm triggers, and we start the scan itself.Â &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;However, with bulk scanning, the process is slightly different:&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/2kXLJ5sSGBbM06H3Ftsrqi/a4440fd0efc7c0271580c6da6f08f814/image9.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1810\&quot; height=\&quot;444\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;In this case, there are no Durable Objects involved just yet; the system simply sends each URL in the bulk scan submission as a new message to the queue.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Notice that in both of these cases the scan is triggered asynchronously. In the first case, it starts when the Durable Objects alarm fires and, in the second case, when messages in the queue are consumed. While the durable object alarm will always fire in a few seconds, messages in the queue have no predetermined processing time, they may be processed seconds to minutes later, depending on how many messages are already in the queue and how fast the system processes them.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;When users bulk scan, having the scan done at &lt;i&gt;some &lt;/i&gt;point in time is more important than having it done &lt;i&gt;now&lt;/i&gt;. When using the regular scan workflow, users are limited in the number of scans per minute they can submit. However, when using bulk scan this is not a concern, and users can simply send all URLs they want to process in a single HTTP request. This comes with the tradeoff that scans may take longer to complete, which is a perfect fit for &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/queues/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Cloudflare Queues&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. Having the ability to &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/queues/configuration/configure-queues/#consumer-worker-configuration\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;configure&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; retries, max batch size, max batch timeouts, and max concurrency is something weâve found very useful. As the scans are completed asynchronously, users can request the resulting scan reports &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/api/resources/url_scanner/subresources/scans/methods/get/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;via the API&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4&gt;Discover related scans and better IOC search&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;The &lt;i&gt;Related Scans&lt;/i&gt; feature allows &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/api/resources/url_scanner/subresources/scans/methods/list/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;API&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a href=\&quot;http://dash.cloudflare.com\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Cloudflare dashboard&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; and &lt;a href=\&quot;http://radar.cloudflare.com\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Radar&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; users alike to view related scans directly within the URL Scanner Report. This helps users analyze and understand the context of a scanned URL by providing insights into similar URLs based on various attributes. Filter and search through URL Scanner reports to retrieve information on related scans, including those with identical favicons, similar HTML structures, and matching IP addresses.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The &lt;i&gt;Related Scans&lt;/i&gt; tab presents a table with key headers corresponding to four distinct filters. Each entry includes the scanned URL and a direct link to view the detailed scan report, allowing for quick access to further information.Â &lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/6yRzKVd0M9sNF1uGOWA1vb/212008b5296ad6df23088571f0602930/image3.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1870\&quot; height=\&quot;678\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;We&amp;#39;ve introduced the ability to search by indicators of compromise (IOCs), such as IP addresses and hashes, directly within the user interface. Additionally, we&amp;#39;ve added advanced filtering options by various criteria, including screenshots, hashes, favicons, and HTML body content. This allows for more efficient organization and prioritization of URLs based on specific needs. While attackers often make minor modifications to the HTML structure of phishing pages to evade detection, our advanced filtering options enable users to search for URLs with similar HTML content. This means that even if the visual appearance of a phishing page changes slightly, we can still identify connections to known phishing campaigns by comparing the underlying HTML structure. This proactive approach helps users identify and block these threats effectively.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Another use case for the advanced filtering options is the search by hash; a user who has identified a malicious JavaScript file through a previous investigation can now search using the file&amp;#39;s hash. By clicking on an HTTP transaction, you&amp;#39;ll find a direct link to the relevant hash, immediately allowing you to pivot your investigation. The real benefit comes from identifying other potentially malicious sites that have that same hash. This means that if you know a given script is bad, you can quickly uncover other compromised websites delivering the same malware.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/3rWKgTrGLW297cVFbH9hSY/4555697b668d90f3df4d740bd91d3116/image7.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1999\&quot; height=\&quot;904\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;The user interface has also undergone significant improvements to enhance the overall experience. Other key updates include:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;Page title and favicon surfaced, providing immediate visual context&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;Detailed summaries are now available&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;Redirect chains allow users to understand the navigation path of a URL&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;The ability to scan files from URLs that trigger an automatic file download&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/5O55W8CLMrlPANpzkPAUY0/35748cb200feb79de6251c79d2be87f9/image2.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1472\&quot; height=\&quot;330\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;h4&gt;Download HAR files&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;With the latest updates to our URL Scanner, users can now download both the &lt;a href=\&quot;https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HAR_(file_format)\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;HAR (HTTP Archive) file&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; and the JSON report from their scans. The &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/introducing-har-sanitizer-secure-har-sharing/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;HAR file&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; provides a detailed record of all interactions between the web browser and the scanned website, capturing crucial data such as request and response headers, timings, and status codes. This format is widely recognized in the industry and can be easily analyzed using various tools, making it invaluable for developers and security analysts alike.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;For instance, a threat intelligence analyst investigating a suspicious URL can download the HAR file to examine the network requests made during the scan. By analyzing this data, they can identify potential malicious behavior, such as unexpected redirects and correlate these findings with other threat intelligence sources. Meanwhile, the JSON report offers a structured overview of the scan results, including security verdicts and associated IOCs, which can be integrated into broader security workflows or automated systems.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4&gt;New API version&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;Finally, weâre announcing a &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/api/operations/urlscanner-create-scan-v2\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;new version of our API&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, allowing users to transition effortlessly to our service without needing to overhaul their existing workflows. Moving forward, any future features will be integrated into this updated API version, ensuring that users have access to the latest advancements in our URL scanning technology.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;We understand that many organizations rely on automation and integrations with our previous API version. Therefore, we want to reassure our customers that there will be no immediate deprecation of the old API. Users can continue to use the existing API without disruption, giving them the flexibility to migrate at their own pace. We invite you to try the &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/api/operations/urlscanner-create-scan-v2\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;new API&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; today and explore these new features to help with your web security efforts.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n            &lt;h3 id=\&quot;never-miss-an-update\&quot;&gt;Never miss an update&lt;/h3&gt;\n            &lt;a href=\&quot;#never-miss-an-update\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-left-5\&quot;&gt;\n              &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n            &lt;/a&gt;\n          &lt;/div&gt;\n        &lt;p&gt;In summary, these updates to Security Level, cipher suite selection, and URL Scanner help us provide comprehensive, accessible, and proactive security solutions. Whether you&amp;#39;re looking for automated protection, granular control over your encryption, or advanced threat detection capabilities, these new features are designed to empower you to build a safer and more secure online presence.
